2a1(rgyud): batheg pa chen po'i mdo// sa so rgyas dang / byang chubs mas
2a2(rgyud): dnga'atham sa cad la ngag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag
2a3(rgyud): gis thos pa dus gcig ni/ bcom ldan 'das ri rab kyi tham
2b1(rgyud): la lnga thams cad kyi mtshan re'i gnas na/ byang chung sems dpa
2b2(rgyud): bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma dang thung so gcig tu bzhugs te/ 
2b3(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das lce dang lnga'i bu rung / lA ma yin dang / 
2b4(rgyud): rlung lha dang / na mkha' lding dang / klu dang / gnod spyan dang / mi 'am
2b5(rgyud): ci dang / srin pa dang / rigs sdug rjes 'chang tha mas cad dang // 
3a1(rgyud): snang ba dang / mi snang ba'im me'i tshogs shin tu mang zhing rgya che ba dpag
3a2(rgyud): slong stebargya lta bdus bskod cing mdun du bangar ras
3a3(rgyud): chos ston te/ de nA rnaMs bya de chub kyi sems nga pa'i se mas dpa
3a4(rgyud): chen po la lag ni rdo rje/ rjerje'i rigs thams cad kyis yongs su
3b1(rgyud): bskor cing rig pa'i tshogs dang / phyag rgya'i tshogs de dag thams cad kyis rig sngags 'chang bye ba phrag du
3b2(rgyud): mas yongs su bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas bar snang las babaso nas
3b3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te// bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba
3b4(rgyud): byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug pa dang // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis
3b5(rgyud): gsang ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la bka' stsal pa/ gsang ba'i bdag po nyi shu rtsa lnga
3b6(rgyud): po 'di rnams ni nga'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo yin no// oM sangs rgyas dang byang chub
3b7(rgyud): sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// oM byang chub kyi sems rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu
4a1(rgyud): phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM kun tu bzang po spyod pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM yid bzhin gyi nor du/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'gog pa med pa shes
4a2(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM skye bar 'gyur go shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rnam par shes pa zad/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'bar ba chen po'i chos
4a3(rgyud): nying / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM brtson 'grus shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM tham cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rdo rje zad brtan
4a4(rgyud): pa'i sems/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thong / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgra'o// oM rang bzhin rnam par dag pa'i chos zhing yis
4a5(rgyud): rnam par dag pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// ma las rnam par sbyong ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM nges par gnod mdzes rdo rje can par/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
4a6(rgyud): pa'i sgo'o// oM 'dod pa la 'dod chags rnam par dag pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM mgyog pa'i rdo rje can/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM hUM zad du 'gro ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin/ 
4a7(rgyud): pa'i sgo'o// oM hrIHshes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo/ oM a zhes bya ba'i sgo// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM a ba hUM/ 
4a8(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa' rnam ma mi shes rab kyi rol tu phyin pa'i slar mi bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi sku'i mchog shes gyi la rol tu byin pa'i sgo yo de 'izhim gshegs bzad kyi gdu
4b1(rgyud): rnam par dag pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi thugs kyi rdo rje/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgol// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ 
4b2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje dang / zad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dang / lha dang / mi dang lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs
4b3(rgyud): pa la mngon par bstod do// / 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa ches bye ba/ theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzog s+ho// rgya gar swA du/ sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya bAkAd+h+wi gu h+ya a lang kAr
4b4(rgyud): byA ho tan+da rA dza na ma/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs bsku dang ga/ sung dang thugs kyi gsang brgyan gyi bkod ces bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dpyad kyi zhabs kyi pad+mo la gus phyag 'cha'o// 'di skad
4b5(rgyud): bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje yis rna myor kyi dbang phyug chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi sku dang
4b6(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rje yis phyag rgya chen po'i dam tshig byin gyis brlabs kyi rdo rje'i sku chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyi sku dang gsung dang thug rdo rje yis rin po che chen po'i cod pan gyi rtse ma
4b7(rgyud): gtsug phud kyis dbang bskur ba brnyed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo yis kyi ting 'dzim chen po dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi sku dang / gsung dang zug rdo yis kyi lnga sngogs pa/ 
4b8(rgyud): chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi sku dang gsung dang thug rdo rje mes mchodapa chen po smra ba'i dam tshig gsang ba dang / de bzhin gsheg pa thaMd kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs ye shes dkyil 'khor
5a1(rgyud): chen po dang tshig de kho na nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes gsang ba chen po'i snying po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
5a2(rgyud): kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi mnga' bdag chen po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kun tu bzang po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
5a3(rgyud): kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes dang med cing mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa na mkha' lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rigs dang / snying po dang // phyag rgya dang / 
5a4(rgyud): gsang sngags dang / rigs pa gnyisu med par 'gyur ba dang / de bzhi na gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po la dga' ba dang / de bzhin ga
5a5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi lhag pa 'i snying po mdzes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje ye shes rgyan chen po bkod pa'i
5a6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po la na mkha'i khams thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje ye shes chen po 'ba' zhig dang thabs gcig tu dazhug so// de'ang 'di lta ste/ sgo mtha'
5a7(rgyud): yus pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / na mkha' sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / a po dza'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / 'gyur ba med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang // 
5a8(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / gzhan yang ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa'i rdo rje btsun mo
5b1(rgyud): stong phrag brgya la'ang 'di lta ste/ mda'i mtshon ma'i lag ces bya ba'i rdo rje bdun po dang / dbang drug la lta ba'i'i ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bdun mo dang / nye bar ni ba'i rang bzhin pas zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rjen du
5b2(rgyud): lta ba'i bzhin pas zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod zla mtshan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brda' sprod pa ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'bri ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rol pa dang ldan pa zhes
5b3(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje bdun po dang / 'dod pa'i mchog ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun po dang / dbang drug gis bde ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dmigs pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun po dang / brang las skyes zhes bya ba'i rdo
5b4(rgyud): rje bdur lo ste/ de dag la sogs pa rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyis yong su bskor cing mdun du bdar to// gzhan yang dpag tu med pa'i rdo rje po nya mo chen po rnams dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ 
5b5(rgyud): de yang 'di lta ste/ snying bskul bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya mo chen mo dang / gdug pa thams cad 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rnga bo nya mo chen mo dang / rjesu mnyes pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po
5b6(rgyud): ro chen po dang / khrag 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya mo chen mo dang / thams cad 'phrog pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya mo chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyas pa'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo nas
5b7(rgyud): dang / yang thabs gcig te/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / dam tshig gsum ldan ces bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / 'jig pa'i yan lag can ces bya ba'i rdo rje
5b8(rgyud): sgo srung ma chen mo dang / thog ma pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo dang / gdul dka' 'dul ces bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srung ma chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo rnams
6a1(rgyud): dang / yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ sku gsung thugs thams cad rdo rje 'ching ba ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen po dang / 'jigs pa'i re'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen
6a2(rgyud): mo dang / gtsigs shing rnam par 'gyur ba'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum 'ching ba zhes bya ba rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / bskal par gnas pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rdo rje bran mo
6a3(rgyud): chen mo'o// gzhan yang dpe med pa'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje dgyes pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / 
6a4(rgyud): kun nas 'babs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / rab tu dga' ba'i rjesu 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen po dang / 
6a5(rgyud): thams cad dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen po lasasogs pa'o// gzhan yang rnam pa'i khams zad rgyas par ga/ nga ba'i rdo rje'i yab rnams dang yang thabs gcig ste/ de nga 'di
6a6(rgyud): lta ste/ 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ces bya ba'i rdo rje yab chen po dang / mkha'agro'i rdo rjes dbang phyug dang / dri yi dbang phyug dang / stug po bkod pa dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / 'dun pa srel dang / skye bo yongasu dor ba dang / legs par
6a7(rgyud): sbyangs pa dang / 'dod pa'i rdo rje dang / gdung ba bskyed pa dang / 'dul bar byed pa dang / gdug pa thams cad sel bar byed pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi mgon po dang / gnas pa po dang / brtse ba can dang / chos chang dang / bskyod pa po
6a8(rgyud): dang / spong ba po dang / 'ching ba po dang / skor ba po dang / de dag la sogs pa rdo rje yab rnam so// gzhan yang mtha' yas pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo 'phrog pa'i rdo rje bra po rdo rje'i tshogs dang thabs gcig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje rlung
6b1(rgyud): zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje me dang / rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa dang / rdo rje chu dang / gzhan yang rdo rje rgyal po chen po bzhi la 'di lta ste/ zhi ba byed pa dang / rgyas par byed pa dang / dbang du byed pa dang / mi shes pa zad zad par byed pa ste de dag la sog
6b2(rgyud): pa'o// gzhan yang mchog tu rgya chen po sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rab tu gnas pa'i mchod pa dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ston pa rtag pa mchog gi mnga' bdag ste/ kun tu bzang po'i sku yis ni// 'jig rten gsu
6b3(rgyud): gyi dkyil 'khor spros// bcom ldan rdo rje 'dziran leg bzhugs/ gsang ba rgyan gyi sbyor bas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed par byed pa'i yum gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dus pa thob ste/ de bzhin gshegs
6b4(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi yang dang lhan cig tu dga' ba'i bde ba rjes grung ste/ 'khor dang bcas pa rnams bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags te/ rdo rje'i glu 'dis mngon par bstod nas zhu ba zhus pa/ 
6b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun dor khyod phyag 'tshal/ rdo rje byung ba khyod la 'dud// thugs kyi rin chen mchog khyod 'dud// chos kyi blo gros khyod la 'dud// chos rnams kun mchog khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs
6b6(rgyud): dgod pa khyod la 'dud// dam tshig mchog gi khyod la 'dud// rdo rje sems dpa' phyags 'tshal 'dung // grags po chen po bdag cag ni// mgon po khyed la zhu ba 'u// sangs rgyas thaMd bskyed byed yum// dkyil 'acwo
6b7(rgyud): gyi ni dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i yum rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thaMd kyi yum rnams de skad
6b8(rgyud): ma sgra gcig/ 'jig rten thaMd la khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di las 'ong ba'i sems can rnams dad par mi 'gyur zhing // rang gi sems yongasu sun 'byir la de ma mthong ba'i chos ma dad pas ra
7a1(rgyud): gi sems yang dag par sun phyung ste/ mnar med pa rnams skyes nas bskal pa steng drag mang por man med pa'i sdug bsngal rjesu 'thung bar 'gyur ro// de rgya lam na ma nar med pa'i sdug
7a2(rgyud): bsngal las grol te/ mi rnams skyes par gyur kyang rnam par 'gyur ba'i bzhin du 'gyuraro// rjes ngas pa rnams dang / blo gros chung ba rnams dang / khyi dang / bya 'og dang / byi la dang / ngag dang / stag dang / glang po che dang / seng+ge'i
7a3(rgyud): nga ro 'dra ba dag tu 'gyuraro// de dang 'dre bar mi bya zhing blta bar mi bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zad bskyed pa'i yum de rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar sems
7a4(rgyud): can de rnams kyi mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' stsal pa/ gang gis 'di'i ming gzung nus yongasu zad par 'gyu'o// bsod nams de'i rgyus de'i las kyi sgrib
7a5(rgyud): pa zad de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi skal ba can du 'gyu ro// de nas de dag yid dga' ba skyes nas yang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das
7a6(rgyud): bstan du gsol/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi rgyus dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyal po sems can thaMd la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir gang ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams kyis dran pa tsam gyi sangs
7a7(rgyud): rgyas kyi byang chub thobs par 'gyuraro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun tu bzang po chen po 'od 'phro ba gsal ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhug so// rang gi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rnams la
7a8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dam pa 'di bka' stsal pa/ dkyil 'khor kun gyis yum gyur pa// stong nyid ye shes nyid bshad// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtogs pa zeng rnam par spangs// 
7b1(rgyud): sems can rnams la phan bzhed pa// gang zhig cung zad bstan par bya// de kun sgyu mas sgyu ma'o// 'gro ba sgyu ma lta bur shes// des na sbru ma lta bu yis// sgyu ma lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bya// namakha'i khams kyis
7b2(rgyud): khyab pa yis// thaMd yum gyis yang dag 'khrugs/ phyi rol yang ni brtag par bya// gang ba'i dkyil 'khor yum rnams kyis/ dben zhing dga' ba'i gnas ni// yid kyi leg par 'dus byas pa// na mkha' la ni thig
7b3(rgyud): gis gang ba// thog mar de yi dam paso// de nas rnal 'byor chen pos thig/ gsang ba'i yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// mu khyud dag gi rnam bdun du// kun nas yongasu bskor bar bya// dbus kyis cha ru dkyil 'khor ni// 
7b4(rgyud): 'khor lo lta bur bri bar bya// kun nas brgyad gnyis mdzes pa ni// dkyil 'khor bzhi yi dbus su'o// 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus ni// pad+ma ze 'bru ldan pa dro// mtshams dang mtsham su 'dab mam
7b5(rgyud): ji lta ba bzhin bstims bcas pas// srang bu lnga las yang da/ 'khrugs// srad bu bani yis nye bar sbas// smra ba na dang ni la dag ldan// rta babs sing ge dag gis brgyan// gdugs dang rgyal
7b6(rgyud): mtshan pa dan sogs// bla res steng du bres pa dang // rin chen rdo rje pad+ma ldan sngon// dpag bsam shing gi lcug mas khyab// bu bzang rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ rgyan 'phreng glang po ldan pa'i ni/ phyi rol gnas te legs
7b7(rgyud): par bri// rtog dang mi rtog rnam spangs te// dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbus ni// gsang brgyan gyi rdo rje bya// mnyam por bzhag cing sgru ba yiste/ sems kyis bri ba nyid bya// de nas lha mo zhal bzhi ma// shes
7b8(rgyud): pha rol phyin dge ba// phyag bzhi pa la spyan yangs ma// phyag gnyis kyis na chos 'chad cing // zhi ba'i g.yas par rdo rje ste// g.yon pa pad+mas rnam par brgyan// dkor dang dmar po cher sngo ba// sngo bsangs rin chen
8a1(rgyud): mchog mdzes 'od// gtsug na rin chen gtsug tor che// gtsug rgyan cod pan dam pa can/ skal pa chen po 'od ldan mo// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klungs// gos kyis lho ni legs
8a2(rgyud): bsgribs pa// bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzum bcas shing // sna tshogs gos ni legs gyon pa// dbu ma'i zhal ras gser gyi 'od// zhabs gnyis dbus 'khor lo ste// mdun na rin chen bdun gnas pa// pad+ma
8a3(rgyud): mchog ldan seng+ge'i khri// zla ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gdan// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro ba// rgyab du nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// dpa' bo de yis bri bar bya// 'di yi mdun du bi bye ba// dpa' bo mtha' yas pa y-i zham/ 
8a4(rgyud): stong phrag du ma'i phyag ldan ma// mtshan nyid thaMd yang dag / dgas// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// phyag gi rje pad+ma 'chang // sna tshogs phyogs rgyas phyag gzhan dkrigs// gtsug
8a5(rgyud): ldan dar gyi cod pan can// dbu brgyan pad+ma'i bzhin ras ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dag la bzhugs// de 'od nyi ma lta bu'i 'od// dpa' bo'i rnal 'byor ldan pa yi// dpa' bo des ni bri bar bya/ 
8a6(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' bdag sgom te// der ni snyems pas 'gro bar bya// dpa' bos lho ru bi byA ba// gshen rje'i 'dab ma mdzes pa la// mchog sbyin namakha' dge ma yang // rin chen khri la legs par bzhug/ 
8a7(rgyud): bzhin ras sngo la spyan dkar ba// 'dzum bcas nor bu'i 'og pog can// mgul rgyan ri chen phreng ba mchog/ rkang gdub gdu bu rin po che// yid bzhin nor bu'i lag pa can// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin dgong
8a8(rgyud): nam// de nas blo ldan rab song ste/ nub tu yang ni de bzhin du// dpal dang ldan pas legs par bri/ chu las skyed ma yid 'phrog ma// dmar po'i gos 'dzin dag pa ma// gtsug na cod pan gyis sbas ma// 
8b1(rgyud): sbrul rgyan sna tshogs lus can ma// dar dang rin chen gyis klubs na// pad+ma 'byed pa'i sbyor ba yis// phyag gi lo 'dab dang ldan pas// zla ba'i gdan la yang dag bzhugs// nyi ma du ma'i snang ba can/ ji ltar rigs pa
8b2(rgyud): bri bar bya// de nas byang du phyin nasu// song ste dpa' bos bri bya ba// mi g.yo bzhin ras grags chen ma// mar gang 'bar ba mtshungs pa mo// dkar po'i dar gyis yang dag klubs// gtsug na nor bu cod pan bzang // 
8b3(rgyud): gtsug rgyan sna tshogs dag gis spras// rdo rje dril bu'i log bkra ma// sna tshogs rgyan dang gos ldan pas// zla ba'i bdan la yang dag bzhugs// 'od kyis gtams pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas 'tshams
8b4(rgyud): kyi 'dab ma la// me tog bdug pa dri ldan ma// rdo rje snang byed/ drag pa ma// mchod pa sngags rig pa yi bris// gzugs sgra dri dang ro dang reg/ rang gi bdag po'i phyog su'o// 'dab ma 'dab mar dzad
8b5(rgyud): du// band dang sgeg dang dbyangs chen mo// gar gyi phyag rgya grags chen po// sngags pas 'bad de bri bar bya// pad+ma las skyes 'dab ma la// theng du ni 'grub pa bri// sgo rnams dag ni
8b6(rgyud): thad la// sgo skyong ba ni rnam bzhi dang // phyi rol du yang lha la sogs// ming ni yang dag bri bar bya// de nas khrus byas lus blugs la// me tog bdug sogs kyis bdug ste// sna tshogs gos ni rab gyon la// 
8b7(rgyud): me tog phreng dang gos gyis brgyan// gtsug phud cod pan dang ldan zhing // mdzes pa'i dar gyis yang dag klubs// rdo rje dril bu lag par ldan// sbyor ba bzang ba'i rnam gzhag gis// de nas thaMd dgug par bya// rdo rje ma mo dka'
8b8(rgyud): thub che// bzlog dang rnal ma'i phyag rgya yi// rdo rje sems dpa' bzlas nasu/ rdo rje'i sbyor bas gar bya zhing // lan gsum du ni g.yas bskor bas// rdo rje ma mo'i dkyil 'khor rnams/ dam tshig ldan pa zed byon// glu dbyas
9a1(rgyud): kyis ni rgyal pos bskul/ rang gi slob ma'i tshogs gar gyis// dreg pa yis ni g.yas dang g.yon// 'gying ba dang ni 'dud par bya// 'dir gshegs 'dir shegs so don mdzad brtson pa po// seras
9a2(rgyud): mi mnga' sangs rgyas tshogs mchog mtha' dag dang // bde gshegs dam pa'i yul gyur srid pa'i bskyed pa po// pha rol don mdzad dus la de ring bab pa lags// cis so de nas de dag rang nyid kyi/ rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'thur
9a3(rgyud): pas byon// mtshan ma dag ni bzang po rnams// dkyil 'khor dag tu blta bar bya// rang ngam gzhan la bab sogs pa'i// mtshan ma ji ltar mthong ba na// de tshe nges par ma me ni// bde gshegs thugs kyi dgod par byon// de nas mchod
9a4(rgyud): yon zhadas bsil cho ga ji bzhin rab brtag te/ de tshe babs pa'i ser bso da nams ldan la bri bar bya// gal te de ni mi smra ba na/ hUM gi yi ge dang // ldan pa'i glu dbyangs kyis ni yongasu bskul ba nyid bya// de nas
9a5(rgyud): shes rab ldan ma bzhugs// slob ma'i gtso bo zal sbyar te// mig la mig dar gyis g.yogs la// rab dga' bdag yin yang dag/ dgar// ma me tha~Md la dmigs te// de ni me tog de bar bya/ 
9a6(rgyud): tog gang le lung gyu ga/ ma dzin de yis gyung/ nas ge'i mas ji bzhin du// sa myong nas brtsams na su// shes pa rol phyin pa bar// rmobs lan pa shad pa bya da tsag so su nas su/ rdzo
9a7(rgyud): yu pa pa dang la pa la/  da dug lags kyi ga rgya shin gyi'i rgyun na/ lal phrul lo//  yang / tan du ma du
9b1(rgyud): spongs pa'i slob ma 'gro// mkha' las rdo rje ji bzhin no// des na bkye dam tshig ni// khyod kyis rtag tu srung bar byos// ma mo kun gyi sdom pa ni// theg pa chen po'i cho gas gnas// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis
9b2(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs te/ rdo rje 'dzin pa thaMd kyis yum rnams kyi dam tshig la bka' stsal pa// rin chen sems kyi dam tshig gis/ rnam pa gsum ni sbyang bar bya// thog mtha' bar gyi sbyor ba yis// chung 'bring
9b3(rgyud): mchog gi dbye ba yis// de 'dra'i dam tshig yang dag pa// sangs rgyas kun gyis bka' stsal to// ji srid sems ni spyad kyi bar// 'bad pa yis ni bsgom par bya// bud med thaMd mthong ba ni// lan gsum du ni bskor nas kyang / 
9b4(rgyud): spyi bor phyag ni byas na su// lan gsum par du gsol ba btab// bdag gi ma khyod bu yin te// ji srid byang chub thob bar du// byang chub yan lag nu ma la// byud ma rang gi 'o mas sbyongs// de nas sbyor ldan pa dge/ 
9b5(rgyud): ba'irtadabang skur pa ni sbyin par bya// gser la sogs pa'i bum pa ru// dri yis chu yi yongs bkang la// dar dang ras sogs gis g.yogs te// me tog chun pos mgul rgyan nas// rinam chen
9b6(rgyud): sman gyis rab bkang ba'i// gcig lhag bcu drug bzang ba la// ma me'i snying po nyid kyis ni// brgya rtsa brgyad du bzlas pa yis// sngags shes pas ni dbang bskur ro// slob ma zhi ba bzang po yis// thog mar zhu ba byas
9b7(rgyud): nas kyang // zhabs gnyis la ni mgos btud nas/ bdag ni che ge mo rdo rje// byang chub sems ni rnam sgom pa'o// slongab dpo ma nabs kyi chu skyes la/ dbang bskur byibyin nub bgyid// bskal ba chen po bdag la stsol// sdom
9b8(rgyud): sa da dru sa dang u stsam pa mas ca kyi/ sa kyi kyi sa rdzu ma da ky-i pa ga kyisas bya ma sa/ 
10a1(rgyud): brtul zhugs bzang po khyod kyi drin// de nas dbang skur sbyor ba yis// rdo rje sems dpa'i gong 'phang gnas// slob ma ye shes rdo rje yi// go 'phangs la ni banag na su// bum pa bza
10a2(rgyud): po gcig gam ni// yang na cu drug dag gam ni// lnga 'am yang na bcu yI ni// dkyil 'khor du ni dbang bskuro// dkyil 'khor gyi mdun du ni// dkyil 'khor pad+ma bri bar bya// pad+ma lo 'dab brgyad pa la// ge ser lte ba
10a3(rgyud): ldan pa bri// de yi dbus rdo rje br-i// sna mtshogs rdo rje 'od zer phreng // de yi mdun du 'khor lo bri// chen po rin chen bdun gyis bskor// lho yi phyogs rin po che// nub tu pad+ma nyid yin te/ byang du ral gri chen po'o// 'bar
10a4(rgyud): ba'i phyeng 'khrugs 'od zer can// grwa yi phyogs ni tha~Md du// me tog bdug pa dri zhim pa// 'od ldan pa ni sa la ba che// sgo dang so ru bzhi nyid do// phyi rol du yang mi 'chi kun// gcig nas gcig tu
10a5(rgyud): rgyal sgrogs pa// bde byed gcir bu'i tshe lugs te// ming tho sa pa dang ldan pa'o// dkyil 'khor de yi dbus ni// slob ma/ bsgrums dang bcas pa bzhag/ chos kyi rang bzhin gtam brjod do// 
10a6(rgyud): de ring khyod ni rigasu skyes// 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po chen// rtog pa dam pa'i dbang phyug pa// thabs dang shes rab ldan pa'i dpal// dag pa'i dbang phyug kun gyi bdag/ rdo rje pad+ma lag byin te// gnang ba bzang
10a7(rgyud): po rab tu sbyin// bu yis bya ba chen po gyis// sangs rgyas kun gyi go 'phangs gnas// der ni sbyor ba 'ongs nasu// gsang ba'i sdom pa sbyin par bya// 'di ni mchog tu dga' ba ste// yum rnams rab tu rmad byung ba'o// 
10a8(rgyud): dusu 'dod pa nyid kyis// dam tshig mchog tu gyur pa'o// brtul zhugs bzang pos ci 'byor pas// de nas yon ni phul byas nas// slob dpon gyi ni zhabs la btud// ma dang chung ma bu mo dang // sring mo sring
10b1(rgyud): mo'i bu mo dang // bu rnams dang ni bdag nyid dang // rgyal po longs spyod gter dang ni// nor dang 'bru dang grong shing rta// glang po rta dang ba glang sogs// ma he dang ni ma he mo// gzhan dang gzhan yang ci 'dod pa// bla ma la ni chen/ 
10b2(rgyud): bos dbus// byang mi bya rdzas kyi mchog/ zad kyang ni dbul bar bya// de nas bcom ldan ma rnams la// rgyun phreng rnams dang bsad gang dang / sgeg dang che 'jo dga' ba dang // rab tu dga' ba'i bde chen dang / 
10b3(rgyud): bza' btung bca' la sogs pa// rnam pa du ma tha~Md kyis// mchod nas gshegasu gsol bar bya// sen kun gyi don dang ni// bdag gi yang ni cher ches mdzad// bde gshegs gang du gshegs pa der// ma mo
10b4(rgyud): bad gshegasu gsol// shes rab ldan pas yon phul te// sleb ma'i mchog dang bcas pa yis// gar byas la// dpa mgor bzhag ste// rims kyis 'gyed dang 'dud par bya// de nas
10b5(rgyud): bzang rnam gnyis te// thed sgrub par byed pa'i mchog/ bdag gi skal bzang stsal nas kyang // rang gi sras kyi gnas gshe gas// de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje
10b6(rgyud): yis yum chen po rnams kyi phyag rgya ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongasu rdzog so// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa zad kyi gsang ba'i yum bcom ldan 'das ma rnams kyi yang gsang ba 'as
10b7(rgyud): pa las byung ba rang rang gi grub pa'i thabs rgyas pa bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces zhuso// shes rab yis mchog sgrubs pa'i// seMs dpa' chen pos gsung du gsol// thabs kyis sen
10b8(rgyud): thaMd kun// sangs rgyas byang chub 'bras thob pa// rdo rje yis mchog gyur pa// rdo rje sku ste rdo rje mchog/ dngos grub kun gyi bde ster ba/ rdo rje chen po gsung du gsol// thugs kyi rin chen ldan pa'i mchog
11a1(rgyud): gzi brjid rdo rje snang ba can// son rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul dang // 'grub pa'i yonan 'byung gsus// sangs rgyas kun gyi rdul 'a che// rnal 'byol chen po dbang phyug che// 
11a2(rgyud): ba'i sbyor bas gar gnas pa'i// dpa' bo chen pos gshad du gsol// las kun gyis ni 'bras bsres pas// sna tshogs byin pa dbang phyug che// seMn rnams kyi yab chen po// sna chags dam pas bsha
11a3(rgyud): du gsol// zhes bya ba so// de nas bcom ldan tag pa'i rgya'o// dam pa'i dbang phyug kun mkhyen pas// gsung mchog na mnga' dang mtshungs pa'i// zab mo yi chos bka' stsal// 'dir sgrub po gang yang med/ 
11a4(rgyud): dngos grub pam ni sru thangs kyang // thaMd rnam par rtog las byung // rnam rtag kyang ni dmigs ma yin// bdag med sangs rgyas rnams kyang med// chos rnams med cing chos nyid med// myur
11a5(rgyud): ba med cing seMn med// de bzhin pa dang ma yang med// bye ba ma/ de cing skyong ba med// 'bras bu med cing rgyu yod min//  ngas spyad med cing zab po med// shes med shes pa po yang med/ 
11a6(rgyud): rnam shes med cing shes da// bdun na na pa ma yin pa/ sa rlung ba' ni// rdzus spyad kyi la jung / de ltar tshus rnams rnams gan// grol nas gas pa sa 'gyur te/ nga ma thu
11a7(rgyud): po 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub bde chen po// zang mo'i chos ni thos pa na// mkhas pa gang zhig dad gyur na// snying po'i phyag rgya sngags rig rnams// gdon mi za bar 'grub par 'gyur// sbyor
11a8(rgyud): ba 'di ni bcom ldan gsungs// thaMd dag par byed pa'i mchog/ gsang ba'i rgyan la legs bzhugs nas// sems can rnams la bstan pa po// de nas yum rnams tshim gyur te// rang byung ba la zhu bzhus
11b1(rgyud): grub pa'i sgrub thabs rab sbyor ba// mnga' bdag rnal 'byor rnams kyis gsungs// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyis yul las kyi dam tshig 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting
11b2(rgyud): nge 'dzin la sgoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// namakha'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de yi steng du ma nyams pa// nam pa'i mtha' klas khyab pa yi// phyogs kun tu ni rab 'phro
11b3(rgyud): ba'o// de yi steng du gzi brjid che// dus mtha'i me dang mtshungs 'dra ga/ de yi steng du sa chen po// gser gyi ri bo dang mtshungs pa// de yi steng du chur shes bya// zla ba gang ba kha ba 'dra// sngags pas cho ga
11b4(rgyud): bzhin du bsam// rin chen bzhi yi rang bzhin bzang // stong blag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi yi// dpag tshad kyi ni tshad tsam pa// gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs bzhi yi rtse mo can// ri bo chen po cog
11b5(rgyud): brgyad pa// dbusu rdo rje'i ri bo mcho'o// de yi steng du rdo rje che// ku na tu phyogs pa yongasu sgom// sngo bsangs mar ga ta // sna tshogs 'od kyis yang dag 'khrugs// de yi steng du
11b6(rgyud): rje che// rtse mo lnga pa rnam par bsam// dkar po shel dang 'dra ba po// 'od zer lnga yis rnam par sbas// de yi steng du rin po che// chu skyes sngon po'i 'dab 'dra ba// sna tshogs 'od zer stong gi phreng // phyogs
11b7(rgyud): bcu namakha' khyab pa'o// de yi gtsug tu pad+ma che// namakha' khyab pa yin ni mchog/ lo ma stong phrag du ma can// lte ba dang ni ze 'bras dkrigs// de yi mdun du nyi ma che// 'od zer stong phrag dus can// de yi
11b8(rgyud): steng du blab mo// dga' pa'i 'od zer ba rabs dkrigs// rnam pa'i khams ni gang ba yin// gzi yin da' bo 'phro ba'o// de yis dbusum me khri/ dus gsum bzhugs pa'i sa sa rgyas kyang / 
12a1(rgyud): yongasu dag pa mkha' 'dra ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'phro ba mo// phyag gnyis ma la thugs zhi ba// bsam gtan spyan ldan bsam gtan yid// bsam gtan mchog
12a2(rgyud): gri phyag rgya yi// ser mo gzhon nu rab bshad pa// dkar po'i gos 'dzin 'dzes pa mo// dkar po yi ni rgyan gyis brgyan// ral pa'i thor tshugs cod pan bzang // gtsug gi nor bu 'od ldan pa// 
12a3(rgyud): yis gdan la mnyam par bzhugs// ba spu rnams kyi rtse bu gnas// rgyal ba rab tu 'phros pa ste// byang chub pha rol son par mdzad// de yi thugs kar rnam bsam pa// yi ge mchog tu mi
12a4(rgyud): 'gyur ba// yi ge rnams kyis yang dag dkrig/ thaMd du/ da ni legs 'phro ba'o// sangs rgyas rnams ni 'dun gnas pa// rab tu thal mo sbyor ba'o// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' rnams// 
12a5(rgyud): rig sngags khro bo'i cho ga rnams ni// chos nyan pa yi chu la du yang // dkyil 'khor du ni bzhag par bya// sgo yi phyogs ni thang du// sgo skyong ba ni bzhi rnar so// sbyin pa la sogs ci rigs
12a6(rgyud): pa ri// bcu drug po'ang bzhag par bya// me tog bdug pa mar me che// ji lta ba bzhin bzhag par bya// lha klu de bzhin gnod sbyin dang // dri za lha min dmyal las byung // 'di rnam zang lhun po la// kun nas yod
12a7(rgyud): su bzhag par bya// de nas me tog phreng ldan 'jug/ dri dang me tog yang dag ldan// gos dkar 'dzin pa dpal dang ldan// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par rgya ni// shes rab 'phro dang lhan cig tu// rdo rje sas
12a8(rgyud): dpa' rjes dran pa// bdag pas de ni dag par bya// shes rab sbyor bas gang nas pas// sgo yi drung du lags 'dod la// glu 'di yis ni spyan drang bya// thugs rje mnga' ba chos kyi dbang phyug sangs rgyas yum/ 
12b1(rgyud): rang gi yang kyi tshogs dang sras dang bcas te byon// skyon cig spyon cig lha dang sring mor bcas mchod pa'i// 'jig rten dbang phyug yang dag byang chub thug mnga' ba// spyon cig spyon cig thugs rje'i bdag nyid
12b2(rgyud): 'jig rten gnyen// chos kyi yi ge bde bar gshegs pas rjes bskos pa// mkha' ltar yongs dag dri med dam bca' dran par mdzad/ ma mo rnam ni mchog glus bskul bas byon par 'gyur// de nas bcom
12b3(rgyud): ldan 'das ma byon par thong nas rang gis me tog gi snyim pa dang mchod yon dang zhabs sil dbul bar bya'o// oM bdag gi mchod yon zhabs bsil 'di// ci bdi bar ni bzhi su gsol// de nas de dang ldan
12b4(rgyud): cig tu// 'dres pa ru ni gyur par bsam// oM sarba ta thA ga ta prad+d+ha dz+nyA na sa ma ya hUM sa ma ya ste// de nas 'di yis brtan par bya ste/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta tsa la sa ma ye ma tsa la ste/ de nas 'dis
12b5(rgyud): mnyes par bya// oM sarba ta thA ga ta/ man san+d+hu sti sa ma ye hUM i h+ye hi dzaHe h+ye hi dzaHde nas dpag tu med pa'i ngo mtshar chen po lta ba'i phyir// oM sarba a ga pu N+Da rem hA b+ha ga bAn
12b6(rgyud): le A raslar sngar s+pha ras rba a ga sa bA yu br-iSh+Ti ma hA bu d+ha sa mu dran tsU hUM a/ 'di yis mamo bskul nasu// sangs rgyas smin na/ 'od pa che// dkyil 'khor ba la slo bar bya// de nas gsang sngags 'ang seM ni// bsngags
12b7(rgyud): sa sa bya/  sa kyisasu mi ma nas gar ba shed pa bzhin du pa la 'ab rdzi mam pa rnams la gtugs ma ngags pa kA pa rgya
12b8(rgyud): b.rabs la'ang gis dang srung ngag stong ba gas spang ba bye'o// de nas las zang kyi rus pa dang / dngos grub zad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas po tog lasags dang / ba' dang lung da dgags/ da kyi
13a1(rgyud): rdza rgyas pa yin/ slob pa'i rgyal po gsug pa / 'tshar los bsgyur pa'i rim pa sa// sbyor ba yis ni yang bsu'o//  rje chen de bzhin pa / las kyi rdo rdo de bzhinan/ 
13a2(rgyud): gags pa lpags kyu dril bu dang // lcags sgrog rnga ya ba dang ni gdugs/ ral gro lag sngar thu ma gnyis// rgyal po'i nye bar sbed pa dang / de la rgyan rnams bzhanas// dkyil 'khor der ni dang bskur// 
13a3(rgyud): rgyal ba'i yum gyos dang bskur ba// las kun byed pa rab tu bshad// dam tshig gam ni sdom pa yang // rang gi slob ma mnyan du gzhug/ zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// dbang dang drag shul spyod pa ni// 
13a4(rgyud): legs par rnam par dag sems kyis// ci 'dod par ni bya ba byos// las rnams kun gyi 'bras bu yang // sbyor ba 'di yis 'grub par 'gyur// de nas btso ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos slar
13a5(rgyud): yang las dam pa rgyas par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// dza lha'i gzugs kyi snod byas la// dkyil 'khor gyis ni
13a6(rgyud): dbusu bzhag// zho dang mar sar 'o ma ni// tsan+dan dmar po dang bsres te// ga pur dang ni ldan byas la// yid la byed pas bzlas te sgrub// zla ba nyi ma gzas bzung tshe// sbyor ba bzang po'i rnam bzhag bya// thog mar meni
13a7(rgyud): spar byas nas// 'bad pa yis ni rlung gi bu// gser gyi snod du bsdu bar bya// ba ru na yau khu bas sbyar// nyi ma dang ri zla ba la// slar yang rdzas de bskam par bya// de nas lho ru lha mo yi// khrag dang sa bon blugs
13a8(rgyud): par bya// de yis myur du rdzas dag ni// 'grub par 'gyur te zi tsa mo med// grub nas thog mar lha mo la// cung zad tsam cig dbul bar bya// de bzhin du ni slob dpon la// skal ba nyis 'gyur dbul bar bya// 
13b1(rgyud): de nas grub pa gzhan rnams dang // rang gi slong mar skal ba bzhin/ de nas byin rlabs sbyor ba yis// phyag rgya dang ni lhan cig tu// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzir gyis// zas kyis sa bon dang ni bza'// skad cig
13b2(rgyud): de la gzugs brjes te// rdo rje sems dpa' lta bur gyur// gang dang gang gi gzugs rnamasu// sgrub par 'dod pa'i sngag pa yis// de dang de yi bsaM gtan gyis// blo gros brtan pas bza' bar bya// 
13b3(rgyud): dang de yi gzugs ni// gdon mi za bar brje bar 'gyur// gzhan pa yi ni rdzas dag kyang // 'di nyid kyis ni bsgrub par bya// mig slar gyis ni mig byugs pas// khor yug tu ni mi snang 'gro// snying la ldong sa
13b4(rgyud): kyis byugs na// yid kyi spyod yul nyid du 'gro// ba bla yis ni lus byugs na// mkha' la nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur// mi sman na ga po blangs na su// nag po'i phyogs la bza' bar bya// 
13b5(rgyud): de yi bshang ba'i mar khu las// dud pa mkhas pas bsgrub par bya// de yis mig la drug nas ni// sangs rgyas kyis kyang mi gzigs shing // stobs ni dpal ldan rdo rje'i mtshon// 
13b6(rgyud): nyid 'gyur rga dang 'chi ba meng // mig sman dang ni ba lang mar// ma he dang ni ra nyid dang // mi yi mig sman nyid dag ni// mkhas pa yis ni blangs na su// sngags pas gzungs ste btso bar bya// mig sman chen po
13b7(rgyud): mchog tu bzang // 'di yis mig la byug na ni// grub pa yid du 'ong bar 'gyur// mi snang 'grub pa tha~Md kyis// blo gros chen po rgyal por 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi sa chen po// nges par thob 'gyur/ 
13b8(rgyud): gzhan du min// rdzas kyi gnas skabs le'u 'di// mtshungs ming chen por nyer bshad do// gos dang gdug sogs ral gri dang // mtshon cha dam pa bsgrub par bya// snying po snying kar byas nas ni// bskom
14a1(rgyud): na myur du grub par 'gyur// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po chekra pad+ma'i sems dpa' bzhin ras mchog/ de yi zhal du byas nasu// de dang ldan pas bskol par bya// mnga' bdag gang gis
14a2(rgyud): dbang phyug ltar// skad cig de la de 'gyur ro// de nyid kyir spyi bo'i char// mchog dam pa bsam gtan bya// skad cig de la mchod pa che'i// sangs rgyas ni de 'gyur ro// de yi spyi gtsug nyid du ni// sna tshog rdo rje
14a3(rgyud): bsgom par bya// de ni kun gyi rgyal dbang po// las kun byed pa'i don grub 'gyur// rdo snying kar bsam par bya// de yi dbusu snying po blta// de nas rdo rje rig pa 'dzin// mnga' bdag rdo rje'i dbang po 'grub// rim

19b4(rgyud): yi 'khor los bsgyur bar 'gyur// bzlas pas mtshan ma ba zang byung na// rnal 'byor pa ni nor chen 'gyur// bar mas gling ni thob par 'gyur// tha ma yi ni khor yug go// zing du ni
19b5(rgyud): bzlas tsam gyis// longs spyod zad par 'gyur ma yin// rgyal po thams cad dbang 'gyur zhing // bud med thams cad dga' bar 'gyur// snying dkar rnal 'byor byas na su// nor bu lag par bcad du
19b6(rgyud): niHnyi ma'i dkyil 'khor lag gnas sgom// myur du rin chen rgyal por 'gyur// phyag rgya 'dir byas gyur pas// rtag tu sgrol bas bsgom par bya// ji ltar 'dod pa'i grub rnyed// rdo rje 'dzin pa ji bzhin no// 
19b7(rgyud): zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas bka' stsal to// de nas sbyor ba ji bzhin du// yum de rnams ni legs byon nas// las kyi dkyil 'khor legs gnas pa// ston pa la ni zhu ba zhus// gang
19b8(rgyud): du rgyal ba kun bzhugs nas// bla na med pa'i don mdzad pa// sems can kun la bde slad du// myur du las ni 'grub pa lags// de nas bac+doMs las thaMd kyi dam pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge
20a1(rgyud): 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyi yum gyi dam tshig dam pa de rnams la las kyi dkyil 'khor bka' stsal pa// rlung gi dkyil 'khor/ 
20a2(rgyud): bri bar bya// de yi dbusu gru gsum pa// de yi steng du lha me bzhag// 'bar ba'i me dang mtshungs pa la// zhal bzhi pa la cher 'jigs pa// mche ba rab tu gtsigs pa'o// thod pa'i phreng ba'i cod pan can/

20a4(rgyud): ma'i zhal ni mdor sdus pa// sna tshogs gtum dang drag pa'i zhal// du ma'i phyag gis yang dag 'khrugs// zhags pa lcags kyu thod sogs dang // rdo rje can gyi sog le 'dzin// zod pas
20a5(rgyud): lus la bres gyur cing // cod par chen pos 'jigs byed mo// gshin rje dpa' bos bri bya ga// mtha' gdong dam pa yi ni ma cho ga/ sngon po 'bar ba'i rang bzhin khros// mgo bo'i phreng
20a6(rgyud): bas rnam par rgyan// zod pa'i phreng ba'i cod pan can// stag gi lhag pa'i sham thabs can// ral gri rin chen thod pa dang // rin chen dbyug gu 'dzin pa'i mchog/ de nas lha mo legs bri ga// pad+ma'i
20a7(rgyud): zhal ma 'jigs chen po// dmar mo phyag na nyi zla 'dzin// bskal pa'i me dang tshungs pa mo// g.yon pa ru ni khro mo che// ma sbyom ma ni ska rags mgul// las kyi rdo rje dri ldan mchog/ mche ba rnam par
20a8(rgyud): gtsigs pa'i zhal// gtsug na thod pa 'jig su rung // rab gtum stobs dang gsal ba mo// 'byor ldan cho ga rig pas bris// phyi rol tu ni legs bri ba// khro bcas 'jigs pa dang bcas pa// 
20b1(rgyud): ral pa'i thur tshugs chen po can// khrag gis gang ba'i thod pa dang // phyag rgya bzang pos phyag mtshan pa'o// de yi byi ru l+la rnams ni// snying pa rab sbyar yi dam pa// thams cad du ni yongasu bzhag/ 
20b2(rgyud): 'jig rten skyong ba bzhag par bya// sgo rnams dag ni thams cad du// sgo skyong ba yang de bzhin du// de nas gtor ma'i cho ga ni// sha bcas btung ba ro dang ldan// de nas go cha bcings gyur pa// thod pa'i
20b3(rgyud): cod pan chen po dang khrag gam chang gis bkang ba 'am// thod pa ldan pas 'jug par bya// thams cad 'grub pa'i ma mo rnams// 'di yis spyani drang bar bya// dkon mtshe gsum la gnod byed pa'i// 
20b4(rgyud): gsang ba'i don du ma mo rnams// di ring nyid dkyil 'khor 'dir// 'jigs chen ma rnams thams cad gshegs// 'jigs pa/ 'i sgra dang cher gtum dang // kha nas 'od zer stong phrag ni// 
20b5(rgyud): mthong ba dang ni thos pa na// mtshan mar yang ni shes par bya// de nas de yis a rag sbyin// ci bder bzhes cig 'jigs mdzad ra// gdug pa chen po gsol bar mdzod// gdug tum
20b6(rgyud): 'jig par byed pa yis// de nas bdag la dbang bskur te// thod par gnas pa'i ro yis ni/ srang tsam gyi ni sha zos nas// ma mo thams cad bsgrub par bya// de nas mngos spyod las rnams kun// dam cig
20b7(rgyud): bsrung ba yis ni bya// dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed dang // bla ma rnams la 'khyal smra ba// rtag tu gsod par lha po rnams// bgyid par bdag ni rje su zung // de nas cho ga de nyid kyis// sleb ma'i dbapa
20b8(rgyud): gzhug par bya// khro bo'i lha la bskul nasu// me tog dmar po dor bar bya// bdag gi me tog dam pa 'di// ci bde bar ni bzhe su gsol// bdug pa 'di ni bzung na su// gsol byed 'di ni gsol
21a1(rgyud): gas nga ni skur bya/ de nas sde'i thos nas// dam tshig 'bad pas 'dzin du gzhug/ rab tu gdug pa'i snying gi lpag bang po dun 'thung zhig hU~M// ma shig za shig sha chen po// btung ba
21a2(rgyud): ba chen po 'thung // gzhon du na ni 'tsho 'gyur te// mkha' 'gro ma dang gza' rnams da // gnod sbyin srin po gtum ze yi// ring por mi thogs rab tu ba// de nas mngon spyod las rnams ni// stong phrag
21a3(rgyud): dag ni bslab par bya// de yi sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor gyis// rang nyid khro bor bzung gyur nas// gnod byed thams cad ba dasad par bya// dgra rnams dzad bza' bar bya// gdug pa thaMd bca' bar
21a4(rgyud): bya// srin po thaMd gzhom par bya// mtha' yas zhal mang sbyor ba yis// bsad dang bzung ba de yis bya// zhal ba ni ma yi sbyor ba yis// thams cad 'gugs pa'i dam dam pa yin/ 
21a5(rgyud): mkha' ba dong ma yis thams cad du// rin po che yi tshogs 'byung // pad+ma'i zhal gyi sbyor ba yis// chang gi dam pa btung bar bya// ma sgrom ma yi sbyor ba yis// sha ni 'gugs pa'i mchog yin
21a6(rgyud): no// na mkha' rengs pa chen po ste// dmag dpung 'byor pa'i dam pa'o// rmugs dang rmongs pa thams cad du// dpyad pa ru ni mi bya'o// sngar bshad pa yi las rnams dang // ma bshad pa la ci 'dod
21a7(rgyud): pa/ bzlas pa tsam gyis kun bya ste// thams cad du ni the tsom med// dur khrod kyi ni bal ba la// dgra bo gzugs ni 'bad pas bya// ming dang spel bar byas na su// ma mo'i ral gris btub par bya/ 
21b1(rgyud): de nas nyi ma bdun na ni// brlab par 'gyur bar gdon mi za// gang lus ji ltar bcad gyur pa// de dang de yi yan lag 'chad// zhal ba zhi ma yi sbyor ba yis// sngags pa mnyam par bzhag pas
21b2(rgyud): bcad// de yi mgrin par zhags pa ni// mkhas pas smos te bcing bar bya// lcags kyus snying khar phug nasu// rlung gis bskyod de drang bar bya// de nas de yi ming bskul nas// de ni shes rab ldan
21b3(rgyud): pas dgug/ dman dang mchog gi dbye ba yis// 'di yis 'bras bu nga yis bshad// mdor bsdus pas ni shes par bya// sngags pa'i rgyal po'i sbyor ba yis she so// de nas bac+doMs ma de bzhin
21b4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad ni// de yis dngos grub gsol mi 'gyur// nye bar 'tshe ba 'jigs rnams dang // gdon dang gnod sbyin srin po bcas// mi zad nad kyis btab na su// shi nas
21b5(rgyud): mnar med nyid du 'gyur// de nas de bzhin dbang bskur/ gyis// dkyil 'khor la bzhag yum rnams kyis// dbang bskur gsang ba'i dam tshig sbyin// gsang ba'i sgrub ma
21b6(rgyud): can du gzhug/ rang yum ma mo'i sa bon gyis// rang gi rnam rtog bdag yum min// lta bus yab gyur sgrubs na ni// nyi ma bdun ni rab tu 'grub// sangs rgyas kun gyi yab ston pa/ 
21b7(rgyud): kun+ta ma dran ye shes spyod yul te// drag po kun dang bde chen po// ye shes kun gyi mchog gi mchog/ shes rab kyis ni thams cad slub// las rgyas pa yi dam pa'i mchog/ bye brag tu ni skul nas// byang chu
21b8(rgyud): na yon gyi/ mas cad du ni 'dags la pa'i// dngas grub thams cad bsrub par bya// shes rab rgyan las dbye bas/ gzugs dang byabs nyid dgagiso// phyag rgya dang ni phyag rgya'i lar// de bzhin kyil 'a pa
21'a1(rgyud): tshig dang // bza' ba dang ni cir spyod pa// gtor la lha ba shos nyid dang ni/ shin tu bde ba'i stan nyid dang // de dang de ni nges par sbyar// dazlas dang bsam gtanas bor ni// rang gi lus
21'a2(rgyud): pa nyid do// gsang sngags dag ni thams cad las// gsang sngags 'di ni rab tu bsngags// tshe 'dir dam pa'i rjes grub cing // gdon mi za bar thob par 'gyur// 'di ni bcom ldan kur rdo rje// ye shes 'byung
21'a3(rgyud): gnas mnga' bdag gsungs// las kun gyi ri sbyor ba yis// 'di ni sgyu mas 'gro la bzhug/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum de rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//

21'a5(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas 'di skad ces pa/ 'astsal to// phyag rgya rtag su yang dag bshad// tha snyad tsam du rnar par brtags// sangs rgyas kun gyi kla klo'i skad// phyag
21'a6(rgyud): rgya thams cad yang dag bshad// 'on kyang mgon po mchog gi brtags// lag pa'i rnam dgod mtshan ma nyid// gang gi yid ches legs skye rnams// dam tshig shes pa'i lha rnams ni// sgrub po rnams kyis
21'a7(rgyud): rab bskul na/ grub pa'i dam pa rab tu stsol// dus las thams cad byon nasu// slar yang gshegs pa nyid du 'gyur/ lag pa zla ba nyi mar bya// shes rab thabasu rab tu brtag/ de nas sngags pas yod
21'a8(rgyud): su sbyar// rang gi sa bon dag gis mtshan// oM pra dz+nyo pA ya sa ma yo ga/ de nas thal mo nges par sbyar// phan tshun rje su rtogs chen po// khu tshur shin tu bzhag par bya// khu tshur bsdams pa lta bur bcing / 
21'b1(rgyud): sau ru ni sbyor bar bya// snying gi dbusu nges par bzung // g.yon pa'i steng du lag pa g.yas// bzhag ste sor mor so sor bya// lag yas sgreng nas phyogs kun tu// 'khor lo'i sbyor bas sgo bar bya// rdo rje sgo ldag

21'b3(rgyud): zad sbyar bar bya// chos kyi las ni chen po byed// de nyid snyam du bskums pa ni// las kyi phyag rgya zhes grags// de bzhin ming med byas nasu// lhag ma rnams ni gdong du sbyar// phyag rgya chen po shin tu ni//

21'b5(rgyud): ma mo de rnams kur// slar yang gtso bo la bstod nas// shes rab chen po rnam bzhi yi// phyag rgya zhu ba rnam par byas// phyag rgya bzhi yi rab kyi mchog/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' grol cis
21'b6(rgyud): gsang ba'i phyag rgya'i yal ga mchog/ shes rab thabs kyis lus bzang ba// gang zhig gsang ba'i rnal 'byor ni// gang gi rnal 'byor pa bde ba// rdzu 'phrul 'phel dang yang dag pa'i// rdzu 'phrul skye ba

22a1(rgyud): gsang ba'i rnal 'byor rab tu srub// de nyid rdo rje lta bur byas// bskyod pas bde ba bskyed par byed// 'di ni chos 'dzin zhes bya ba'i// phyag rgya gsang ba sgrub pa pa'o// g.yon/

22a4(rgyud): bcing bar bya// 'di ni gsang ba sdams pa'i rgya// yis sdems pa rab tu 'grub// thams cad rdo rje ltar rdo// de bzhin bskyod cing bskor bar bya// de 'di gsang ba rab tshim pa// tshim pa'i don ni ster/

24a1(rgyud): gsol ba btab cing bskul ba'i tshig nyid kyis thugs la bzhag nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor bsgyur ba chen po rab tu sim pa bde ba la
24a2(rgyud): longs spyod pa rnam par dbyings pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byin gyis brlabs te// bde ba chen po 'khor los bskur ba la rab
24a3(rgyud): tu gnas nas nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje rnams la rab tu phyung ngo // dkyil 'khor snga ma bzhin bris la// de yi lte bar 'di dgod do// rdo chen po bsan+ta pa// 'dod pa'i dbang phyug dag dang
24a4(rgyud): ldan/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi yang // kun gyi thog mthaHrab byung ba// de la sogs pa'i rim pa yis// thams cad kun tu brtags par bya// pad+ma'i lo martsibs la ni// 
24a5(rgyud): gi chos dang rab tu spel// ma mo rnams ni thams cad kyis// mtsho da pa la sogs rab tu brtag/ sgo ru sgo ba yongasu brtag/ sgo yis phyi ru sgo skyong ba/ btsun mo lhan cig spyod bcas

286b1(rgyud): na mthong ba de dang ba thob par 'gyur ro// de nas rdo rje 'dzin pa sgrub par 'dod na khro chu'i lcags kyi rdo rje sor bcu drug pa ngos gnyis ka rtse gsum pa tsan ngan dmar
286b2(rgyud): pos byugs la cho 'phrul gyi zla ba'i tshes gcig nas brtsams te ras bris la mchod pa rgya chen po byas la nyi ma re re bzlas pa ba'o// de nas nyal mchod pa rgya chen po byas nas
286b3(rgyud): mar me brgya tham pa sbar te/ ku sha'i chun po la nye bar 'dug la rdo rje lag pa gnyis kas bzung nas ji srid 'bar ba de srid du bzlas nas de bzung bas 'khor dang bcas pa rig pa
286b4(rgyud): 'dzin pa'i 'khor los bsgyur ba thob par 'gyu ro// de ltar 'khor lo dang mdung la sogs pa'i mtshon cha rnams dang / gos dang mchi la lham dang / tshangs skud la sogs pa rtog pa
286b5(rgyud): gzhan gyi cho ga yang bsgrub par bya'o// snga ma bzhin du dngos grub gsum 'thung ngo // de nas nor sgrub par 'dod na seng lde nga gi yam shing rnams zho dang mar gyis skrag
286b6(rgyud): nas stong phrag brgyad bsregs blugs byas na nor stsol bar 'gyuraro// rgya mtshor 'bab pa'i 'gram du song na tsan dan gyis sngags pa'i pad+ma rnams stong phrag brgyad cu chu bo la bskur
286b7(rgyud): na pad+ma'i phung po dang mnyam pa'i nor thob par 'gyuraro// lha dbang du bya bar 'dod na a ka ru'i yam shing rnams zho dang sbrang rtsi dang mar gyis btags nas bsregs blugs byas
286b8(rgyud): na dbang du 'gyuraro// gsum po des btags pa'i 'bras ba sregs na sngags mi zad par 'gyur ro// gnod sbyin dbang du bya bar 'dod na gsum gyis btags pa'i
287a1(rgyud): gu gul gyi ril bus bsregs blugs bsregs pas dbang du 'gyuraro// mya ngan med kyi yam shing gis ni gnod sbyin mo dbang du 'gyuro// rgyal po la yung
287a2(rgyud): kar gyi 'asreg blug byas na rgyal po dbang du 'gyuraro// rgya mtshor 'bab pa'i chu klung gi 'gram du song nas pad+ma 'bum phrag gcig sbyin sreg byas na dpal 'dus
287a3(rgyud): nas nor stsol ba 'am yul phyogs gcig pa'i rgyal srid ster ro// de nas 'bum phrag gsum byas nas byin nas stengs kyi bdag por 'gyur/ 
287a4(rgyud): 'bum phrag lnga byin na 'dzam bu gling gi bdag por 'gyur// lha ma yin gyi bu ga'i sgor ras ris bzhag nas 'bum phrag gsum bzlas na sngags thams
287a5(rgyud): cad 'byung ste dogs pa med par zhugs na bcud kyis len la sogs 'byung bar 'gyuraro// de nas de nyid du gnas na khyab 'jug gis 'khor los
287a6(rgyud): 'jigs pa 'byung ngo // yar ngo'i tshes gcig nas brtsams te dza ti'i me tog stong phrag brgyad du bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs kyi mthe bor reg par bya'o// 
287a7(rgyud): ci sring du zhabs kyi mthe bong las 'od zer byung gi bar du btags na sgrub pa po'i lus de ma thag tu mi snang zhing dbu skra lcang lo 'khyil bar 'gyuraro// 'khor dang bcas pa 'dzin
287a8(rgyud): pa'i rgyal po thob par 'gyur te bskal par gnaso// sa lu pad+ma mdab ma brgya pa gcig bris te de'i steng du 'dug nas stong phrag bzlas nas gzhi gar gnas pad+mar
287b1(rgyud): gnas te 'khor stong dang ldan pa bskal par gnas so// de nas gter blang bar 'dod na gang na gter yod par de ru bum pa skud pa nag pos bkri sa la tsan ngan gyis
287b2(rgyud): thug la chus bkang ste/ stong phrag brgyad du mngon par bsngags nas der bzhag par bya'o// sa degs nas chu yis sa la gtor la zhu gang tsam
287b3(rgyud): sa la brkos te blang bar bya'o// de nas seng+ge sgrub na grog mkhar gyi sa la seng+ge byas la gi'u wang gis byugs la dkyil 'khor du bzhag ste// mchod
287b4(rgyud): pa chen po byas la ci srid du g.yo ba'i bar du bzlas na seng gar 'gyur te rgyab tu zho na pas skra li ba 'khyil bar 'gyur zhing bdag nyid snga ltas thob nas lo kI
287b5(rgyud): phrag gcig tu 'tshe'o// 'jam dpal 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i rtog pa gsungs pa'i cho ga 'di bsgrubs na de ni myur bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das
287b6(rgyud): kyi de skad ces bka' stsal nas zad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag thams cad bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod de// rje su yi rang nas
287b7(rgyud): stan las langs nas song ngo // 'phags pa khro bo'i rgyal po chen po mi g.yo ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs dpag tu med pa
287b8(rgyud): pha rol gnon pas 'dul bar gsungs pa zhes bya ba'i rtog pa rdzogs s+ho// // mi nyag rgyal po'i bka' lung gis rgya gar
